LING TSOS KHA SNA TSOGS YUG NYI SHU, GRVA CHAS

LUS GANG, GA-YU DANG SPOS SHEL CHEB RE, SOG KONG GNYIS, SKE
THAG, LTAG DZAR, GONG RNA, ZANGS CHEN GCIG ,JA 'KHOR DRUG ,THA
KO; RTA GNYIS, MUS GNYER BA DGER SLONG BSKAL BZANG CHOS DBANG
NAS KHA BTAGS, GRVA CHAS LUS GANG, GSER ZHO

BRGYA DANG DRUG CU RE BRGYAD, MCHOD RDZAS SU GSER SRANG NYI SHU
RTZA LNGA LAS GRUB PA'I MCHOD KONG LEGS PA GSER ZANGS KYI STEGS
BCAS, DNGUL SRANG NYIS BRGYA, SPOS SHEL RDOG CHE BA, GSER BAD,
GA-YU DRUG DMAR MTHEB MGO CAM RDOG GNYIS

DANG DRUG DMAR RDOG CHE LEGS GCIG ,BAL GA-YU RDOG CHE BA, BYU RU
CHE BA GNYIS DANG KHROM DZAR GCIG ,ZANGS KHAL BCU BDUN DANG NYAG
BCU, ZANGS SHU KHRI BCAS, MAR KHAL NYI SHU RTZA LNGA, BUR LTANG
GNYIS, BYE RIL LTANG GSUM, LCAGS GZER

RING THUNG NGO GRANGS CHIG STONG DGU BRGYA DANG BCO LNGA, LCAGS
GA-YAB NGO NYI SHU RTZA LNGA, DKAR ME'I THEBS SU 'BRI GA-YAG CHE
CHUNG BRGYA DANG BRGYAD, DGA' LDAN RAB RGYAS GNYER PA YE SHES
RKYA MTSO NAS GSER BRGYAD RDO GCIG ,RGYA DNGUL SRANG BRGYAD,

RTZE 'KHOR DRUG

NYI SHU ;SPOS SHEL RDOG CHE BA, ZANGS KHAL GNYIS NYAG BRGYAD,
BAL LCAGS NGO BZHI BCU ZHE GCIG ,SPEL KHANG DGE SLONG GIS SRING
MO BSOD NAMS SGROL MA'I CHED PHRA RGYAN DU DMIGS GSER GA-YU MU
TIG SOGS KYI RGYAN CHAS DANG GON PA

BCAS DNGUL SRANG DRUG BRGYA DANG GCIG ZHO GANG RTZIS, GZHAN YANG
RANG RANG GI 'BYOR PA DANG BSTUN PA'I DNGOS 'BYOR GYI MCHOD
SPRIN SBRO BA PO DU MA BYUNG YANG DE RNAMS ZHIB PAR BRJOD NA HA
CANG GIS YI GE MANG BAR 'GYUR ZHING, MDOR BSDUS TZAM

ZHIG SMOS NA RGYUN SDOD DRUNG 'KHOR GRAS MGON KHANG DBU MDZAD

GNYEN, MCHOD DPON PA DRUNG RAM PA YE SHES BKRA SHIS, PHYAG PHYAG
PA TSOGS GSOG PA BLO BZANG MKHAS

MCHOG ,ZHUS DAG PA LHA KHANG GRVA TSANG GI BLA MA DKA' CHEN CHOS
MDZAD DANG DKA' CHEN BLO BZANG BSTAN 'DZIN, BLO BZANG BSKAL

MKHAN RNYING YE SHES MTHA' YAS, DKA' CHEN BLO

BCU ZHE LNGA, RAS YUG BRGYA DANG DRUG CU RE LNGA, RTA SUM CU
RNAMS

TE DNGOS PO RNAM GRANGS SHIN TU MANG BA 'BUL MI BYUNG BA RNAMS
'DIS 'DI LTAR PHUL TSUL SOGS RE RE NAS BRJOD KYIS MI LANG ZHING,
SKU GSUNG THUGS RTAN DANG GONG MA CHEN PO NAS STZAL BA'I NOR
BU'I RIGS DANG RIN PO CHE'I SPYAD PA RIN THANG GZHAL DU MED PA

SOGS RGYA MTSO'I GLING PHRAN GYIS MTSON THAG RING PO'I YUL NAS
PHUL BA SKAM GSHER LA GNAS PA'I SROG CHAGS DANG LJON SHING DANG
'DZIN MA DANG RGYA MTSO CHEN PO LAS BYUNG BA SKYE BO PHAL MO
CHES MTHONG BA LTA CI THOS PA'I YUL TZAM DU'ANG MA GYUR PA RNAMS
GONG

DU PHUD, DE PHYIN GSER DNGUL RTA NOR GOS DAR SOGS DNGOS RIGS LA
GONG PHAB KYIS, DNGUL THOG TU BSGRIL BAR DNGUL SRANG BZHI 'BUM
CHIG KHRI LNGA STONG NYIS BRGYA DRUG CU RE LNGA ZHO GSUM SKAR
LNGA BYUNG BA RNAMS LAS MCHOD PA'I RGYUR 'OS PA RNAMS KYIS, SKU
GDUNG

STONG MCHOD DANG BRGYA MCHOD SOGS RGYA CHER SPROS, MCHOD SDONG
GI SKU RGYU DANG NANG GZHUG DANG PHRA RGYAN DU 'OS PA RNAMS
KYANG DE DANG DE DAG TU SMIN BA SOGS KYI SGO NAS CHA SHAS PHRA
MO TZAM YANG,

CHUD MA GZON PAR DGONGS PA YONGS SU RDZOGS SHING 'PHRIN LAS KYI
'JUG PA RGYUN MI CHAD PA'I CHED RNAM DKAR KHO NA'I RGYUR SMIN PA
BSGRUBS TE DGE LEGS KYI 'JUG NGOGS YANGS PAR BYAS SO, ,'DIR
SMRAS PA, LUS CAN 'DI KUN 'BAD PAS BSGRUB DGOS PA'I,,

LAS KHAB LEN RDO BA DANG, ,PHRAD TSE SPRIN BZHIN MI 'DU'I RANG
DBANG CI, ,DAD LDAN RNAMS KYI YID KYI CHU MTSO LAS, ,'ONGS PA'I
DNGOS 'BYOR MCHOD SPRIN 'DI TZAM ZHES, ,TSAD BZUNG NOR 'DZIN
RDUL BZHIN

CHES DKA' YANG, ,MDOR BSDUS RAGS RIM TSUL DU LEGS PAR BKOD, ,DE
LTA'I TSIG PHRENG CHU 'DZIN RGOD PA'I DBYANGS, ,RNA BAR LHUNG
TSE DAD LDAN GTZUG PHUD CAN, ,SPRO BA'I GAR BYED SNGON BYAS DGE
BA LA, ,YI RANG MNGAL GYI PHUNG POS LCI BAR SHOG, CES RJE BLA MA
SRID ZHI'I GTZUG

DPAL BZANG PO'I ZHAL SNGA NAS KYI RNAM PAR THAR PA NYI MA'I 'OD
ZER GYI ZUR 'DEBS SHEL DKAR ME LONG ZHES BYA BA 'DI NI, RJE BLA

KYI THA SHAL CHOS SMRA BA'I BTZUN PA 'JAM DBYANGS BZHAD BA DKON
MCHOG 'JIGS
